        "body": "Someone in the content team wants to use the extension but uses screen magnification. This causes the extension window to fall off the screen. Because the height is set you can't scroll.\r\n\r\n![image](https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/233676/37041556-63137b90-2154-11e8-8689-1b344c9825a9.png)\r\n\r\nThis PR attempts to remedy the issue by setting the height of the extension if the user's browser window is lower than 600 (the max height of the popup).\r\n\r\nWe now gain a scrollbar on the popup but that's an acceptable price to pay.  \r\n\r\n## Before\r\n\r\n![screen shot 2018-03-06 at 15 38 48](https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/233676/37041602-81762ace-2154-11e8-9644-b276ff93d704.png)\r\n\r\n## After\r\n\r\n<img width=\"1213\" alt=\"screen shot 2018-03-06 at 15 38 46\" src=\"https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/233676/37041611-8864aea0-2154-11e8-86dd-f141dbee4c8c.png\">\r\n",

        "body": "This adds a button to the plugin for showing meta tags in a banner at the top of the page. It can be used to see what's being sent to google analytics, and what search engines see when crawling the page.\r\n\r\nIt's equivalent to this bookmarklet: `javascript:(function()%7Bvar d %3D document.createElement(%27div%27)%3Bvar x %3D document.getElementsByTagName(%27title%27)%5B0%5D%3Bvar msg %3D %27<p><strong>title (%27%2Bx.innerHTML.length%2B%27):</strong> %27%2Bx.innerHTML%2B%27</p>%27%3Bvar ms %3D document.getElementsByTagName(%27meta%27)%3Bfor(var i%3D0%3Bi<ms.length%3Bi%2B%2B)%7Bif(null!%3D ms%5Bi%5D.getAttribute(%27name%27))%7Bvar c%3Dms%5Bi%5D.getAttribute(%27content%27)%3Bmsg%2B%3D%27<p><strong>%27%2Bms%5Bi%5D.getAttribute(%27name%27)%2B%27 (%27%2Bc.length%2B%27):</strong> %27%2Bc%2B%27</p>%27%3B%7D%7Ddocument.body.insertBefore(d,document.body.firstChild)%3Bd.innerHTML%3D%27<div style%3D\"border:2px solid %23000%3Bbackground:%23ffc%3Btext-align:left%3Bpadding:1em%3B\"><a href%3D\"%23\" onclick%3D\"document.body.removeChild(document.body.firstChild)%3Breturn false\">remove</a>%27%2Bmsg%2B%27</div>%27%3B%7D)()`\r\n\r\nThe design is not amazing, but I'd rather render this on the page than try and fit it into the popup, because there can be a lot of them, and there is some overlap with information that's already in the popup, but I want to make it clear what's a meta tag and what isn't.\r\n\r\n<img width=\"1406\" alt=\"screen shot 2018-01-11 at 16 23 22\" src=\"https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/87579/34835122-d44ad760-f6eb-11e7-93ce-9f70f3c9348a.png\">\r\n\r\n\r\nTrello: https://trello.com/c/TDeqykiP/106-add-gov-a-lytics-to-the-govuk-toolkit-chrome-extension",

        "author_association": "CONTRIBUTOR", 
        "body": "This PR allows the Chrome extension to show different bucket names than just A and B. Now that we are adding functionality to `govuk_ab_testing` to rename variants, we need to allow the extension to show those. In order to know what variants we can choose from in a given A/B test, we've added a new data attribute to the analytics metatag called `data-allowed-variants` which lists the valid values. If no data attribute exists (for backwards compatibility), we default to `A` and `B`.\r\n\r\nHere are the dependencies:\r\n- [ ] https://github.com/alphagov/govuk_ab_testing/pull/45\r\n\r\nAnd the related PRs that need this change:\r\n- [ ] https://github.com/alphagov/collections/pull/346\r\n- [ ] https://github.com/alphagov/govuk-cdn-config/pull/54\r\n\r\nPart of: https://trello.com/c/S5jp2jih/179-setup-technical-implementation-for-a-b-testing-the-blue-box\r\n\r\nHere is how it looks in development:\r\n\r\n![custom-variants](https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/416701/26973454-9ca84d60-4d0e-11e7-82d3-133469c4b505.gif)\r\n",

        "body": "This fixes issues like this:\r\n    \r\n1. Visit an A/B test page on Integration.\r\n2. Set the bucket to B. If this happens to place you in the B bucket, everything is consistent, and the extension works as  expected.         "body": "This fixes a bug which caused the extension to create an extra cookie named `ABTest-Example`, rather than updating the value of the original cookie.\r\n\r\nThis is because the extension assumed that the cookie path is always the root path, which isn't always true.         "author_association": "CONTRIBUTOR", 
        "body": "Make the A/B test buckets interactive, so that a user can select the version that they want to see. This works by appending a custom HTTP header to the request, which will only work against origin servers - it will be overridden by Varnish configuration if the request passes through the CDN. A future commit will add the same functionality using a cookie, which will work with the CDN.\r\n\r\nNote that the selected A/B buckets are not persisted when the browser is closed. I expect this will be fine for our purposes, which is to view different versions of the page during development in Dev and Integration. We can always add persistence if it turns out to be useful - it just didn't seem worth adding it now, but let me know if you disagree!\r\n\r\nThe Production version of this will use cookies, which _will_ be persisted because we'll be setting the value of a cookie.\r\n\r\nhttps://trello.com/c/jra1OClm/320-make-it-easy-to-test-experiments-in-non-prod-environments",

        "author_association": "MEMBER", 
        "body": "This adds a bunch of useful links to the popup.\n\n![screen shot 2016-06-07 at 12 46 46](https://cloud.githubusercontent.com/assets/233676/15856712/2a81a2c0-2caf-11e6-9de3-cc468b80e677.png)\n- An Edit-link that leads to the publishing application. For some applications we can infer a deeplink from the content_id (like collections-publisher). For others we either link to a prefilled search path (publisher) or link to the publishing app main page.\n- Link to content-tagger (where anything can be tagged) and search-admin (where you can see what raw information rummager holds)\n- Links to the rendering app was already available in the popup, but we now use the content item for this. This means that the link is also available on pages that 404, 410 and 5XX. Previously this link was based on a meta-tag which wouldn't be present on clobbered error pages.\n- A similar link to the GitHub of the publishing application. In some cases this needs some mapping, because the `publishing_app` in content store isn't always the repo name. Make a PR if you find more exceptions.\n- Link to the content schema on GitHub.\n- A link to the brand new publishing-api debug page, which is initially only available in development (alphagov/publishing-api#345).\n\nThe way we generate these links is by fetching the content-item from the content-store when the user opens the popup. This means a slight delay between opening and the extension populating the menu.\n\nI've re-organised the file/js layout to make it all easier to understand. The best way to review this may be by looking at the entire `/src` directory.\n",
